just done some revision on the theory of gaps.

for those interested:

There are four basic kinds of gaps:

1.common gaps

2.breakaway gaps

3.runaway gaps

4.exhaustion gaps

If you ever wondered what causes gaps in price charts and what they mean?
http://stockcharts.com/school/doku.p...nd_gap_analysi

Hope this helps,

--- 帖子 #2464 ---
Among dozens of systems I have come across, this one is the simplest, easiest, most effective and reliable.

No need to buy expensive "Black box" systems.    No need to fret about complicated patterns, set ups or calculations.    Just download Meta Trader Platform from FXDD (Live or Demo), and insert the prescribed indicators.

No need to Sit in front of monitor all day, putting unnecessary stress on your blood pressure.    From Sunday to Thursday, around 16.30 to 17.30 pm EST, just scan your favourite Pairs (or all the pairs available on FXDD) and note down the likely candidates for Full Strength as well as Secondary Strength potential Trades.    Prefer Full Strength Trades and enter.

Be patient.    If there is no trade one day, don't push your luck.    Wait for another day.    Simply enter the trade, when all conditions are literally met and there is reasonable room for the pair to move in the direction of your trade (before price hits some major Support or Resistance).

This routine of minimum effort, easy to follow system and simple discipline of not taking any "Weak" trades, will, in time, bring you impressive profits without too much heartache and panic attacks.

Good Luck and Good Trading.

--- 帖子 #2490 ---
Hi All

Xirtam. . .Here is the set file for EURCAD I am using ATM. . .
Attached File(s)   eurcad.zip

< 1 KB
|
361 downloads

Regarding when to 'take your profit', I do not use the 'close on oppposite signal option'. I use TS and SL only, this is 'tailored' to each pair I am running. By using only a SL and TS I am only deciding how much to risk on each trade and NOT limiting the profit by using a set TP.

No, I do not use previous candle to determine SL and TP for each pair. What I used when I set up this account is Average True Range (ATR). For each pair I included on each 4hr chart the ATR(100). I then used a SL and TS ABOUT 2 times the the 4hrATR(100). All other inputs for each pair is the same as the above preset file. When I originally setup the SL and TS I intended to redifine the TS and SL on a weekly basis but I have fallen behind on this intention. However I can say that I find most pairs will show up in the range of 150 to 250 pips range for the TP and SL.

Thanks to Ash and RR for the great system and EA.

--- 帖子 #2539 ---
Sounds like you are talking about secondary trades per the rules. Why do I say that?

You will never have a reversal of the PSAR and still be in a position unless you have your stop set higher/lower then the first bar of a new reversal. Take a look at the rules and formula behind the PSAR.

I set all stops at the high/low of the initial bar (per the rules, first trades).

--- 帖子 #2545 ---
Scott, if one was long, and the system signalled short, then one has a number of options. There are no hard & fast rules for AshFX Daily. One could either:

a) Quit the long, and go short.

b) Stay long, but go short as well (essentially hedging to an extent)

c) Ignore the long signal, and stay short.

d) Exit the long, and don't go short.

Now, depending on the circumstances, EITHER ONE of those could be a good decision, especially the last one - remember, you don't have to always be in a trade. This is not a stop and reverse system.

Having said that however, generally speaking, options a) and b) are the most viable.

I made a few trades on this system which I started using about a month ago.  After a big hit I decided to start filtering the signals using 150 SMA and only taking trades according to the overall trend.

Trading Record

Second strength long EUR/GBP on 10/8/08 good for +365 pips.  My first half was closed out at +365 pips and my stop that was set for breakeven was hit.

Second strength long on 10/14/08 EUR/USD I was stopped out for -373 pips.  I blindly followed the rules of the system and took a long signal in a massive downtrend which was against my better judgement.

Second strength long on 10/14/08 CHF/JPY I was stopped out for -330 pips.  Again, this long was against the trend and against my better judgement.

After these two losses I decided that I would try to only take first strength trades following the trend due to the economic crisis around the world.

11/03/08 - Long signal for USD/CHF.  The 150 SMA was trending up and there was no major resistance so I took the long.  I set the stop to the day's low at -282.  I'm currently up +111 pips with a first target of 282.

So over a month I took four trades

Long EUR/GBP  +362

Long EUR/USD -373

Long CHF/JPY -330

Long USD/CHF +111 (still open, will be +282 if I win)

So right now I am -230 pips over a month of trading.

If I win the USD/CHF that is still open I will be at -59 pips.

Keep in mind this is taking 2 second strength trades that were against the trend and my better judgement.  I was impatient and couldn't wait to make trades which is why I took these signals and went long in a massive downtrend.  If I had filtered these 2 signals with the 150SMA I would be +362 and +111 for a total of +473 at this time, +644 if I win the open USD/CHF.

I really like the system, but you need to use common sense to filter out the signals and you will be profitable.  I'm not sure if blindly following the signals makes you profitable.  Could someone clarify this?

I don't know why you said "in a timely manner". Your not paying for the system. People reply when they get around to it and if they want to.

Note the name of the thread. It is a daily system as originally presented. If your friend has better results on a 15 minute chart you should talk to him and decide on your own how to trade the system. Some people have used it on a 4 hour chart.

The system was originally tested on FXDD. That is the main reason to use FXDD for the signals. The other reason (in my mind) was so we could compare signals in the thread. If you like the system I would suggest running it on 3 MT4 platforms with different server times. Compare the results. Just because Ash originally tested and developed it on FXDD does not necessarly mean that is the best platform for the daily signal.

FXDD's status with the regulators is harder to define. FXDD has a 'pending' status with the NFA. I don't know if they will complete.  NFA ID: 0397435 if you want to go to the NFA site and look up the principals. http://www.nfa.futures.org/basicnet/...d=0397435&rn=N

The important thing to remember is that you do not need to trade this system with a FXDD live account. You can use a demo FXDD account to get the daily signals and then use your broker of choice. One that you feel is safe, secure, and fair.

--- 帖子 #2576 ---
The Spread is the difference between Ask/Bid for a given pair. For example if you examine the XAUUSD on FXDD the spread is 85 pips, this means when you enter the Trade on this pair you start with -85 pips.

Basically they have a number of outter Bands and a central Middle Line , When prices reach these Outter bands there is meant to be 70% to 90% probability of bouncing back towards the middle line. Hence if we only trade at these pionts eg await for the price to touch them then await your Setup of AO,AC & Parabolic you should be in a more profitable trade.

--- 帖子 #2645 ---
I've tried out many, many systems (same as all the other 'would be traders' out there :-) and I always come back to this one because of its ease of use and its 'set and forget' characteristics. Must confess that I've found it somewhere else on the internet (without the stochastics, only the AC, AO and PSAR) and added a MACD to it. It's one of a few systems that seem to give consistent, longer term profits, although only since a couple of months; might have to do, for the bigger part, with my own improved trading abilities, but you should still give it a try.

Before I open any trades, I look at correlated pairs and after getting some idea of overall trend I look for entries on the H4 charts (retracements - also use the MT4 Fibonacci retracements tool for this). Be aware of support/resistance area's on your charts (zoom out, as to view several days at the time) and don't get in too quick - don't be one of the herd, who gets tricked in to false breakouts by the market makers...). The 'round numbers' area's are of special importance too and I avoid getting into a trade when price hovers around them, up and down 20 or so pips.

Don't know if you're new to trading, but thought I'd give this general advice for all new traders who might come across this thread...

Cheers and good luck!
